NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

NOTICES
PUBLIC NOTICE
FORM No. 155
[See rule 329]
MEMBERS’ VOLUNTARY WINDING UP
Notice convening meeting of Contributories
Notice is hereby given in pursuance of Section 496 of the Companies Act, 1956 that a General Meeting of the members
of the above named Company will be held at No. 88/89, Kuppuswamy Street, Golden George Nagar, Nerkundram,
Chennai-600 107 on Monday, the 23rd day of March, 2012 at 11 O’ Clock in the morning, for the purpose of laying down
liquidator’s account of his acts along with the audited statements, in relation to the winding up of the company.

Chennai,
2nd March 2012.

J SUNDHARESAN,
Liquidator of Multizip Private Limited.

CHANGE OF NAME
I, R. Gopikrishnaa, biological son of Thiru S. Ravichandran, residing at 67/A, North Saliya Street, Korainadu,
Mayiladuthurai-609 001, by way of this public notice inform that Shri P.R. Varadarajan (late) and V. Gunasundari (late), has
legally adopted me, as their son on 29th December 2005. By way of a Registered Deed as Document No. 206/2005, on the
file of Sub-Registrar Office, Mayiladuthurai. My adopted father P.R. Varadarajan passed away on 27th February 1998 and
mother Mrs. V. Gunasundari passed away on 1st February 2007. Hereafter, I shall be known as V. GOPIKRISHNAA.

Mayiladuthurai,
2nd March 2012.

R. GOPIKRISHNAA.
